        <h2 class="date-header">
         <span>
          Friday, July 5, 2013
         </span>
        </h2>
        <div class="post">
         <h1>
          Hotels : North Mal Atoll : Maldives : Reethi Rah, Maldives
          <br/>
          <span class="st_sharethis_large" displaytext="ShareThis">
          </span>
          <span class="st_facebook_large" displaytext="Facebook">
          </span>
          <span class="st_twitter_large" displaytext="Tweet" st_via="realvelvetcouch">
          </span>
          <span class="st_pinterest_large" displaytext="Pinterest">
          </span>
          <span class="st_googleplus_large" displaytext="Google +">
          </span>
          <span class="st_tumblr_large" displaytext="Tumblr">
          </span>
          <span class="st_blogger_large" displaytext="Blogger">
          </span>
          <span class="st_myspace_large" displaytext="MySpace">
          </span>
          <span class="st_stumbleupon_large" displaytext="StumbleUpon">
          </span>
          <span class="st_reddit_large" displaytext="Reddit">
          </span>
          <span class="st_digg_large" displaytext="Digg">
          </span>
          <span class="st_email_large" displaytext="Email">
          </span>
         </h1>
         <div class="post-body">
          <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
           <img border="0" height="427" src="http://cdn.media.kiwicollection.com/media/property/PR002804/xl/002804-03-villa-with-private-deck-over-water.jpg" width="580"/>
          </div>
          <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
           Hotels : North Mal Atoll : Maldives : Reethi Rah, Maldives
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Supreme and private luxury amid nature's tropical magic, One&amp;Only Reethi Rah, Maldives resort is a jewel among a string of coral atolls, lagoons, and white sands. The experience is privacy, warmth and moments of magic  a promise of utter contentment fulfilled.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Serene and Private Maldives Resort. One&amp;Only Reethi Rah offers 130 private resort villas well separated along the shore, either on the beach secluded by lush tropical greenery, or set above the clear, protected waters of the lagoon. Designed in an elegant contemporary style, these are among the largest resort villas in the world.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <b>
            Contact Reethi Rah, Maldives
           </b>
           <br/>
           <a href="http://reethirah.oneandonlyresorts.com" target="_blank">
            Website
           </a>
           |
           <a href="https://www.facebook.com/OneOnlyResorts" target="_blank">
            Facebook
           </a>
           |
           <a href="https://twitter.com/OOResorts" target="_blank">
            Twitter
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://www.youtube.com/OOResorts" target="_blank">
            YouTube
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/ooresorts" target="_blank">
            Flickr
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://pinterest.com/oneonlyresorts" target="_blank">
            Pinterest
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://instagram.com/ooresorts" target="_blank">
            Instagram
           </a>
           |
           <a href="https://plus.google.com/108579723560631460328/posts" target="_blank">
            Google+
           </a>
           <br/>
           Address : North Mal Atoll, Maldives | Phone : + 960 664 8800
           <br/>
           <br/>
           <b>
            Sources
           </b>
           :
           <a href="http://cdn.media.kiwicollection.com/media/property/PR002804/xl/002804-03-villa-with-private-deck-over-water.jpg">
            Reethi Rah, Maldives Photo
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://reethirah.oneandonlyresorts.com/">

           </a>
